commit 0515e02fecdf054fe374a9fd50937cd927a36048
Author: Navneet Singh <navneetsingh0693@gmail.com>
Date:   Wed Feb 3 22:42:08 2021 +0530

    Issue #3134077 by ronaldtebrake,jochemvn, bramtenhove - Drupal 9 compatibility (#2144)
    
    We have added drupal core compatibility to our info.yml files to show all our custom work is compatible by using
    core_version_requirement: ^8.8 || ^9
    
    We have ensured to remove all deprecated code which is removed from Drupal 9. The replacement code is compatible with Drupal 8.9 as well so untill all our contributed modules are Drupal 9 ready, we are still installing Drupal 8.9.
    
    We have added phpstan as a github action, to make sure we wont be using any deprecated code anymore either. All new code will be ran at lvl 5 strictness as well, to ensure our code is also hold to a higher standard.
    
    Co-authored-by: jochemvn <jochemvn@gmail.com>
    Co-authored-by: ronaldtebrake <ronald@goalgorilla.com>
    Co-authored-by: Bram ten Hove <bram@getopensocial.com>

commit 9cec25038753196584128c491f4a3c0bcb117f16
Author: Serhii Myronets <serhii.myronets@lemberg.co.uk>
Date:   Wed Oct 14 16:24:24 2020 +0300

    Issue #3171512 by agami4, Kingdutch: Add title to SVG elements for all type of the teasers (#2023)
    
    * Issue #3171512 by agami4: Add title to SVG elements for the all type of the teasers
    
    We ensure that all information in a teaser that is conveyed visually is
    also available without being able to see the visual components.
    
    * Move event listener to body to prevent 'clickable' in voice over
    
    When a click event handler exists on a parent of an element that is not
    the body, OS X Voice Over (and possibly other screenreaders) will
    announce any element selected as "clickable". This is quite disruptive
    when going across teasers that contain non-clickable text.
    
    Delegating the execution of the click handler to the body solves this
    issue and no longer makes a string such as "Open Group" announce as
    "Open Group, clickable".
    
    In this case this is the right thing to do since the menu should only be
    closable by clicking on the content on mobile, when the menu is open.
    For screenreaders there are other ways to properly close the menu after
    opening it.
    
    Background: http://www.pauljadam.com/demos/voiceover-clickable.html
    
    * Apply screenreader fixes to non landing-page and sky teasers
    
    Co-authored-by: Alexander Varwijk <alexander@getopensocial.com>

commit f026dc2c84364980a3ff5649a61f46d756f1ec7f
Author: Alexander Varwijk <Kingdutch@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Mon Oct 12 13:45:31 2020 +0200

    Issue #3175829 by Kingdutch: It's unclear that dropdown menu items are expandable (#2027)
    
    We look at the Bootstrap example and add the missing `aria-haspopup` and
    `aria-expanded` attributes. The `aria-haspopup` attribute indicates to
    assistive technology that there is a submenu present. The
    `aria-expanded` attribute indicates the state of that submenu. The
    `aria-expanded` attribute was already updated by the included JavaScript
    but the initial `false` state was missing from the Twig rendered markup.
    
    In addition we add the `role='button'` to indicate to screenreaders that
    this is a menu button which makes it clearer that the button can be
    pressed for more options.

    Issue #3108608 by ronaldtebrake: Render the form--coment with a possibility to add classes, in this case we are adding classes so ajax_comments understands whenever we are replying on a reply. in Open Social replying on a reply means we use the normal comment add form, with a mention which is submitted similar to a reply. commit 6e3a4ee02f32060a600e72d401622e7451b199fd
Author: Alexander Varwijk <alexander@getopensocial.com>
Date:   Thu Oct 8 14:10:17 2020 +0200

    Issue #3134488 by Taco Potze, collinm, ronaldtebrake, Kingdutch: Image with Post does not work after removing the image
    
    It appears that an AJAX call introduces a random string after the
    selectors that are used in the script. This breaks the script. We're
    unable to trace the source of this change but we can make the script
    more robust.
    
    We only check for the start of data-selector. We also limit all queries
    to the current concept in an attempt to make this work when there are
    multiple forms on the same page.
    
    The CSS is slightly updated because it appears that the line is no
    longer needed but instead causes issues. The comment was correct that
    the stylesheet was only loaded after the image is shown, but it's not
    unloaded when the image is removed. This caused a visual bug that was
    present until a very early (<1.7) version of Open Social.

commit 3a4e193087519c954fb0fef59d6c63e89d375d6f
Author: Alexander Varwijk <Kingdutch@users.noreply.github.com>

    Issue #2947667 by ok_lyndsey, Kingdutch: Style skip to content so it is easily visible on each page (#2004)
    
    The style is borrowed from Drupal.org. For the colors we've chosen to
    use the navigation active link color as it's usually different from the
    navbar color itself. Additionally it has a matching text color that
    should be configured by platform users to something accessible. This has
    the highest chance of resulting in a skip link that is styled to the
    platform styles while being accessible.

commit 8587d04d7407f23d25c45169c866d9b412afe2d3
Author: Alexander Varwijk <alexander@getopensocial.com>
Date:   Tue Apr 28 17:27:39 2020 +0200

    Force update graceful-fs to fix gulp@3
    
    graceful-fs monkeypatches the Node fs module which no longer works in
    newer versions of Node. It's not currently feasible to update gulp to a
    newer version. However, the only change between graceful-fs 3 and 4
    should be that it no longer monkeypatches `fs` which shouldn't matter
    for the way gulp used it.
    
    More information on this can be found here: https://stackoverflow.com/a/58394828/576060

commit 4edfaef39e244ff584be275faf73790263689950
Author: Alexander Varwijk <alexander@getopensocial.com>
Date:   Thu Apr 23 11:24:07 2020 +0200

    Fix template suggestion for comment upload field group
    
    The structure of the render array produced by the Field Group module has
    changed which meant that our template didn't apply anymore causing
    comment uploads to be inaccessible.
    
    This commit changes the logic for adding the file suggestion, relying on
    the consistency of the ID of the field group. `substr` is used because
    a properly generated ID will get a `-*` number suffix when it's rendered
    on a page multiple times, so an exact match may break in that case.

    Issue #3096602 by Kingdutch: Fix admin toolbar and menu z-index fighting
    
    We've been adding z-index fixes to the menu for the admin toolbar.
    However, changing the z-index of the menu causes it to go under page
    elements which wreaks havoc.
    
    This commit looks at the underlying cause and stops trying to change the
    menu but only changes the admin menu.
    
    Unfortunately we do have to force the menu into relative positioning to
    ensure the menu's aren't positioned on top of eachother.

commit 960c8c21d4ec445b5e513c0cd7fcc1466f9746f1
Author: Alexander Varwijk <alexander@getopensocial.com>
Date:   Tue Mar 31 15:58:21 2020 +0200

    Issue #3119327 by Kingdutch: Apply styling for accept/decline buttons for group invitation
    
    This removes the styling for the sky theme for the group join button.
    The `transform: uppercase` was removed from Open Social quite some time
    ago for a11y reasons and should not be re-introduced. Additionally the
    `.btn-block` class exists for full width blocks. Using this per button
    instead of forcing it from outside allows the dropdown for the
    accept/join button that is desired.
    
    The dropdown styling is also applied to the old flavour.

commit e7aa3ed7a8db22fbb021d0e4d6f502a34dfb0eb6
Author: Alexander Varwijk <Kingdutch@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Mon Mar 16 12:23:01 2020 +0100

    Issue #3111959 by chmez, Kingdutch, Ronaldtebrake, ribel: As a CM I want to customise filtering options in the custom content block (#1714)
    
    * Implement dependency between fields
    
    * Create a new plugin type for implementing dependencies between fields and add the first instance for topics
    
    * Replace form fields for selecting a content type and filtering field by database fields
    
    * Move filtering query to a method of new plugin type
    
    * Add field to plugin definition for entity type ID
    
    * Use the main theme instead of the admin theme for pages for creating and editing block
    
    * Replace the bundle label field of plugin definition by the bundle ID field
    
    * Add configuration of new fields to already enabled the module
    
    * Fill in fields for plugin ID and plugin fields in existing blocks
    
    * Restore the previous position of the database service between injected services to the builder service
    
    * Issue #3111959 by chmez: Use entity base table instead of entity data table as the main table of the filtering query for has access to fields for sorting
    
    * Issue #3111959 by chmez: Read a configuration from the code of update hook instead of reading configuration from YAML-files
    
    * Update only blocks with an empty field for plugin ID
    
    * Update a few blocks during on iteration of the update hook
    
    * Add deleted phrases to the translations.php file
    
    * Add comments to some parts of the code
    
    * Rename topics variable to entities for the social-content-block template
    
    * Apply default theming for the form actions section
    
    * Fix bugs and fix dashboard usage of content list block
    
    The block wouldn't render on layout builder pages because the correct
    hook was not implemented.
    
    Additionally, implementing that hook exposed some bugs. When no fields
    were selected, the `empty` value of the field selector would not
    actually be empty but would be interpreted as a special field. This is
    fixed by checking for that field name, although this will break if a
    field named `all` is every added. So it's probably better to just make
    the field be actually empty.
    
    Additionally a query alter would fail if there were no filters selected
    because it attempted to do a join with an `IN` clause without and
    values. This is not allowed in a SQL database.
    
    * Delete empty fields before sending them to the plugin
    
    * Add checking group content type
    
    * Leave empty the field of the selected filter when all filters have been selected
    
    * Add template file for content list block
    
    This removes a custom template file for the content list block and
    replaces it by a normal block template file.
    
    It also begins the theming of the new small teaser look and feel for
    topics/events/etc.
    
    * Change text-muted color to #555
    
    The text muted color of #777 often doesn't pass WCAG standards.
    Darkening it slightly fixes this.
    
    * Add content list block and small teaser styling
    
    This changes the output of the small teaser and the content list block
    for the new styles. The image is added as an element to be displayed.
    This still requires a configuration update.
    
    * Update view mode for new small teaser style.
    
    This adds the update hooks and configuration changes for the layout
    changes made to the Small Teaser style for all group types and
    topic/event node types.
    
    It relies on the Update Helper module to apply these changes. This
    module will be added in another PR. Update hook dependencies will need
    to be set to make that work.
    
    * Add filter-fields on the create/edit block page automatically from the plugin definition
    
    * Change position description field
    
    * Add checking if the plugin management service exists before call it in the override service
    
    * Improve update-files for completely hiding fields on the entity pages
    
    * Add checking if the content of the block already exists
    
    * Fix social_event CUD names
    
    The names of the files was accidentally changed during a commit clean-up
    but these should match the update hook name that they're executed in by
    convention.
    
    * Fix dependency on update helper update hook
    
    Social Event update hook 8802 uses the update helper module but this is
    not enabled until social_core_update_8805 so depending on
    social_core_update_8802 could cause issues.
    
    * Fix update-files for completely hiding fields on the entity pages
    
    Co-authored-by: Roman Salo <frs.daddy@gmail.com>
    Co-authored-by: Alexander Varwijk <alexander@getopensocial.com>
    Co-authored-by: Serhii Myronets <serhii.myronets@lemberg.co.uk>

    replaces it by a normal block template file.
    
    It also begins the theming of the new small teaser look and feel for
    topics/events/etc.
    
    * Change text-muted color to #555
    
    The text muted color of #777 often doesn't pass WCAG standards.
    Darkening it slightly fixes this.
    
    * Add content list block and small teaser styling
    
    This changes the output of the small teaser and the content list block
    for the new styles. The image is added as an element to be displayed.
    This still requires a configuration update.
    
    * Update view mode for new small teaser style.
    
    This adds the update hooks and configuration changes for the layout
    changes made to the Small Teaser style for all group types and
    topic/event node types.
    
    It relies on the Update Helper module to apply these changes. This
    module will be added in another PR. Update hook dependencies will need
    to be set to make that work.
    
    * Add filter-fields on the create/edit block page automatically from the plugin definition
    
    * Change position description field
    
    * Add checking if the plugin management service exists before call it in the override service
    
    * Improve update-files for completely hiding fields on the entity pages
    
    * Add checking if the content of the block already exists
    
    * Fix social_event CUD names
    
    The names of the files was accidentally changed during a commit clean-up
    but these should match the update hook name that they're executed in by
    convention.
    
    * Fix dependency on update helper update hook
    
    Social Event update hook 8802 uses the update helper module but this is
    not enabled until social_core_update_8805 so depending on
    social_core_update_8802 could cause issues.
    
    * Fix update-files for completely hiding fields on the entity pages
    
    Co-authored-by: Roman Salo <frs.daddy@gmail.com>
    Co-authored-by: Alexander Varwijk <alexander@getopensocial.com>
    Co-authored-by: Serhii Myronets <serhii.myronets@lemberg.co.uk>

    problematic because we want to style the block a certain way for the

    with theme suggestions.

commit f91d65a8d2fbfd95375d99b27f240234636eaaf4
Author: Alexander Varwijk <alexander@getopensocial.com>
Date:   Wed Feb 12 13:49:01 2020 +0100

    Remove redundant entity load
    
    The layout builder calls the preprocess hook with an unsaved entity.
    This is fine because we already have the entity from our variables
    array. However, it suddenly becomes apparent that using the entity you
    have to load the new entity isn't needed. It's also problematic if the
    entity is not yet persisted because then it can't be loaded.

commit 48fa8d14bba7313a7bc15ca75ddf33a3673b8d10
Author: ronaldtebrake <ronald@goalgorilla.com>

commit 24f7a82335004fd6424c03b05643d2b442f16f60
Author: Alexander Varwijk <alexander@getopensocial.com>
Date:   Wed Jan 22 09:44:10 2020 +0100

    Add back jQuery UI styles in SocialBase
    
    We used to remove some styles for jQuery UI. Probably because they broke
    some things. However, we can not figure out what actually breaks, but we
    do know that without these styles we can not properly support the layout
    builder.
    
    To remedy this the styles are added back in and the socialbase/modal
    styles that create extra conflicts are removed from automatically
    extending the jquery dialog library. To secure two cases where this
    removal could possibly break things the library is manually added if the
    dialog library is present.
    
    This should preserve backwards behaviour as much as possibly while
    allowing the layout builder to function without issues.

commit d3aef0837f7d8f22605268bb093114a3fcd3573d
Author: Alexander Varwijk <alexander@getopensocial.com>
Date:   Wed Jan 22 09:44:10 2020 +0100

    Add back jQuery UI styles in SocialBase
    
    We used to remove some styles for jQuery UI. Probably because they broke
    some things. However, we can not figure out what actually breaks, but we
    do know that without these styles we can not properly support the layout
    builder.
    
    To remedy this the styles are added back in and the socialbase/modal
    styles that create extra conflicts are removed from automatically
    extending the jquery dialog library. To secure two cases where this
    removal could possibly break things the library is manually added if the
    dialog library is present.
    
    This should preserve backwards behaviour as much as possibly while
    allowing the layout builder to function without issues.

    Issue #3072888 by jaapjan, xinyuma, NatashaSchon, Kingdutch: sorting on search content (#1474)
    
    * Issue #3072888 by jaapjan, xinyuma: add sorting options with Better Exposed Filter to the content search.
    
    * Issue #3072888 by jaapjan: install better exposed filters module.
    
    * Issue #3072888 by jaapjan, xinyuma, NatashaSchon: wording of sort options.
    
    * Move search filter blocks into separate functions
    
    The edits we make to search filter blocks are all standalone so it's
    more readable to move these into separate functions and just call the
    right one with a switch statement in the main alter implementation.
    
    * Issue #3072888 by Kingdutch, xinyuma, jaapjan: visually separate sorting and filtering options.
    
    We add the visual separation of sorting and filtering to show users that
    these are different options. The filter title is added in CSS because
    it's not easy to reliably change the form structure.
    
    This commit also undoes the changes to the block template because it
    breaks the sorting form behaviour (the field would be rendered outside
    of the form).
    
    * Issue #3072888 by jaapjan, Kingdutch: prefixes for dependencies.

    a theme.

commit 8c9160af1c4f7854fb0de1ce2bf1b7b5b692a75b
Author: Alexander Varwijk <alexander@goalgorilla.com>
Date:   Mon Jan 28 14:39:58 2019 +0100

    Fix visible user menu in non-chrome browser
    
    In Firefox (and possibly Safari and IE as well) the user menu was
    present because it was in the same z-index plane as the button that is
    used for the search background. By giving the button a non-zero z-index
    it will be displayed above the other navbar items.

commit 2cc0aa42f6636148fc29ceeac1417e3cf21692b3
Author: Alexander Varwijk <alexander@goalgorilla.com>
Date:   Mon Jan 28 14:35:23 2019 +0100

    Fix flex width adjustment in non-chrome browsers
    
    Flexbox has an interesting behaviour when the min-width is not set in
    Firefox (and possibly Safari and/or IE as well).
    
    The related spec is here: https://drafts.csswg.org/css-flexbox/#min-size-auto

commit bf5b83e8ad7e5a6a5a22780da9c089cbfbe5748f
Author: Alexander Varwijk <alexander@goalgorilla.com>
Date:   Mon Jan 21 15:58:05 2019 +0100

    Set-up React rendering under the search block
    
    Adjusts the styling for search to work when more items such as the
    search suggestions field are added. Also adds weights to the search form
    to ensure that it can be properly sorted without rearranging its
    contents.
    
    Finally adds the compiled module javascript as a library and attaches it
    to the search form.

commit a0d59d5b65f2d175901a3bb822f0de09bfea1a88
Author: Alexander Varwijk <alexander@goalgorilla.com>
Date:   Tue Jul 31 16:36:42 2018 +0200

    OSSUPPORT-579 Improve the usability of login and register screens
    
    If a user is sent a link to a page that he/she can not access and
    he/she does not have an account yet then the default login page of
    Open Social is pretty useless.
    
    When the social login module is used then those buttons are displayed
    inside the login/register card which turns out as a weirdly nested
    card.
    
    This commit cleans up the login page by adding a link between
    login and sign up screens so that users can easily navigate between
    them while preserving the post-login destination parameter.
    
    Furthermore the commit moves the social buttons into their own
    cards.
    
    Finally a configurable text is added both for normal/social login
    as well as register. This allows site-managers to guide users
    during these procedures as needed. By default only the sign-up
    screen has a text configured.
    
    A follow-up issue to clean up the configuration and make it reusable
    is here: https://www.drupal.org/project/social/issues/2989522

Author: Alexander Varwijk <alexander@goalgorilla.com>
Date:   Mon Jun 11 09:29:32 2018 +0200

    Convert old template array to a Drupal core render array
    
    We transform the render array that was used for the custom template
    file to one that can be used with mostly Drupal core render elements.
    
    We add one UnwrappedContainer render element that provides us with
    a container without a div. This ensures that we can have multiple
    child elements in a <li> element without the list_item element
    rendering multiple <li> elements.
    
    This provides a good basis for simplifying it into our own render
    element.

commit 78ef01cdefd7f5a1e580cd2e33cccd65d8206118
Author: Alexander Varwijk <alexander@goalgorilla.com>
Date:   Wed Jun 13 09:37:40 2018 +0200

    Issue #2979293 by Kingdutch: Change download hover text
    
    Wether a file opens in the browser or is downloaded depends on the
    file format and the browser configuration (type, addons, etc) of
    the user. Currently the text "Open file in a new window" is used
    which gives a user the expectation of seeing the file in a new
    window even if this is not necessarily the case.
    
    We change the text to prime the user for the possible behaviours
    of the browser.

commit 09e60cc72c5ba18f55130bf45ba6dc64692251d5
Author: Alexander Varwijk <Kingdutch@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Wed Feb 14 14:21:26 2018 +0100

    Issue #2944720 by Kingdutch: Profile anonymous theme suggestion is too important
    
    The following commit that introduced Public Group support added a theme hook for profiles that is used when anonymous users view the page: https://github.com/goalgorilla/open_social/commit/8c71ef1e59125a18f87a83.... However, because that suggestion is simply added to the stack it is used over any other custom profile displays that may be used. This breaks existing sites.
    
    The solution to this is to add the suggestion only after the suggestion it supplements. This way the original importance is maintained and any anonymous template takes precedence over it's non-anonymous counterpart.
    
    In a solution for this I've extended the hooks to add anonymous versions for all suggestions that are implemented by the profile module which provides some additional flexibility.
    
    This results in the following list of file name suggestions:
    
    ```
    <!-- FILE NAME SUGGESTIONS:
       * profile--305--teaser--anonymous.html.twig
       * profile--305--teaser.html.twig
       * profile--305--anonymous.html.twig
       * profile--305.html.twig
       x profile--profile--teaser--anonymous.html.twig
       * profile--profile--teaser.html.twig
       * profile--profile--anonymous.html.twig
       * profile--profile.html.twig
       * profile--teaser--anonymous.html.twig
       * profile--teaser.html.twig
       * profile--anonymous.html.twig
       * profile.html.twig
    -->
    ```

    Rename all Alter, Process and Preprocess socialbase classes
    
    This commit removes the unnecessary prefix from all classes. That
    function is already fulfilled by PHP namespaces.
    
    There were some inconsistensies in filenames and classnames
    capitalisation. These inconsistensies have been left for what they
    are because existing sites might be using them.
    
    This should provide a backwards compatible solution to using the
    proper classnames and all prefixed classes have been marked
    deprecated with a reference to their replacement unprefix class.
    
    No tests should need changing.
    
    Also fixes a few coding style issues in the files.

commit 432deb6545b6ef8013a938f30302d7c1c887cb6a
Author: Alexander Varwijk <alexander@goalgorilla.com>
Date:   Mon Sep 18 17:38:52 2017 +0200

    Issue #2909681 by Kingdutch: Call parent::preprocess for socialbase alter plugins
    
    We dictate that subthemes extend the SocialBase plugins so that
    our functionality at least gets all the required theming variables
    it requires. The function `PreprocessBase::process` in the
    Bootstrap theme does quite some heavylifting for us that a
    subtheme plugin might depend on. We should therefor ensure that
    this function is always called whenever we overwrite the function
    in our socialbase theme.

commit 6edb00b4ecb5817e0efb7a08618b442969cf01ff
Author: Alexander Varwijk <alexander@goalgorilla.com>
Date:   Tue Aug 22 11:44:51 2017 +0200

    Improve margin targetting of comment paragraphs
    
    It looks better if the like button is flush against the bottom of
    a comment. To achieve this the margin-bottom of paragraphs in
    comment text is set to 0. This has the drawback that long
    paragraphs become very difficult to read.
    
    This commit changes the targetting of the margin-bottom to be only
    for the last paragraph in a comment. This ensures that for both
    single paragraph and multi-paragraph comments the like button is
    flush against the last paragraph. However it ensures that spacing
    between multiple paragraphs is retained.
    
    This changes nothing for short, one paragraph comments.
